The place was packed so that was a good sign. The Sandwich Board had a lot of choices of bread but by the time I got there they only had two choices of bread left. So I got a bread that I really didn't want. I wanted sliced Sour Dough but I got a White Roll. I really loved that they use Boars Head Deli products! Even though I got a White Roll and not Sour Dough the Sandwich was good because turns out they they do give you somewhat a good amount of Meat in there Sandwiches, so I was really happy about that! The only thing that I wasn't to Crazy about was that my Sandwich was Really "Dry"! They put VARY LITTLE amount of Mayo, Deli Mustard and Italian Dressing on my Sandwich. Don't know if that's how they normally make them or if that's just how mine came out? I Really like my sandwiches with just a bit extra more Mayo and Mustard on my sandwiches. So that's why I gave them 4 Star's out of 5.</review>

< Review>
We recently discovered this place and have been back a couple of times. They have nice selection of hot and cold sandwiches and salads... my husband has tried the turkey with avocado, the pastrami and hot roast beef. I've had the cold roast beef all three visits, but on different breads. Everything we've tried has been freshly prepared, tasty and service is fast. Their food is a little pricey, but you definitely get what you pay for. When we want a good deli sandwich again, Ventura Sandwich Company will get the call.</Review>

<rating>5</rating>< text>
I've been going to color me nail for almost ten years. Even when I moved up the peninsula I hated every salon I tried up there. I only get pedicures and haven't asked for artwork in years, but it's always the best value for my money. It's changed management a couple of times but it's mostly the same friendly, caring women that work there. They no longer offer personal tool sets with your name like they used to but I'm okay with that. It's always clean and they are usually careful to show you opening newly sanitized tools in front of you. The massage chairs are mostly fat friendly, as I'm a size 26 with 62" hips and they fit me perfectly, is say if you're closer to a 32 it might be tight. I've never encountered any day hating remarks or negative body comments here in general. Sometimes other clients may carry these conversations but it's pretty rare. They play a pleasant mix of music from classical, easy listening, pop and edm...seriously, it's great because you never know what will come on. I'm a music nerd so this is great for me. I always call ahead but rarely make appointments. They do have very busy times but want to help everyone so you may have to wait if you don't phone ahead. A quick call and like today I called at 3:30 wanting a 4pm slot and she said they're busy can I come at 5. Worked out perfectly for me and I was out by 6 sharp. They carry OPI and Essie for regular polishes. They carry all of the major gel/shellack brands, like a ton! They do good gel manicures. They have different levels of pedicures and manicures. I love the Queen pedicure wish includes a 15 minute massage (they set a timer and show you), scrub, mint mud mask, brief hot Stone massage, hit towel wrap and a good creamy lotion,  hot parifin wax for you feel and callous softener. It's so relaxing and right now only $35. You can pay with cards but they generally prefer cash and definitely tip in cash!</text>

<text>We arrived the day after xmas. Our gracious host Tom greeted us as we came in and escorted us to our site overlooking the river under magnificent valley oaks. In addition to their various batches of wine, balsamic vinegar and olive oil from neighboring farms were available in the tasting room. We purchased their Zinjo, a spicey red as well as a Sauvignon Blanc. The Zinjo was delicious. We're waiting to open the white wine this evening.

The estate has a well maintained trail that weaves among the hundreds of acres of vines and the riparian landscape. In one small meadow, we sat a spell in Adirondack chairs under the canopy, a welcome if too brief respite from all covid worries.

The estate is less than 15 minutes from historic downtown Lodi and it's small shops and restaurants.

Visit Heritage Oak. You won't regret a single minute.

< review>
I was just driving by this burger joint.  Then my friend said they had good burgers.  What's a GOOD burger? I thought... So instead of asking him. I drove in.
They had a full menu over the counter, i could see cars pull by their drive-thru, they didn't seem to be waiting to long... Star!  I had to ask the lady for the house specialty, she looked confused so i just went with a burger combo.
We ordered two of the same, when she rang us up the total was around $8bucks and change, cool.  As I was about to reach for my wallet to pay for my order.  She walked away...  It was the price for both combo's!... Boom! Star!  It didnt take long when she called our number. Two average sized burgers and pair of steaming hot fries, we already had our drinks.
Ok.. the fries were piping hot! Fresh out the fryer.  Burgers has noticeably fresh veggies, and a freshly cook patty I took a bite... Hmmmm.  I said "this is a good! Burger"...Star!  All in all there's nothing bad about this place, also nothing super.  That's it.

My friend wouldnt stop raving about the fountain drinks, he swore their syrup mix for the soda was unlike no other place in L.A....  IDK
So just in case he hits this post some day...Star!
...just cause you wouldn't stop talking about it Doug Stewart.<//review>
